select elements I found that multi selects were not part of the Gumby UI demo.  I checked the CSS files and found no styling other than \'.picker select\'.  Prefacing the &lt;select&gt; elements with the \'picker\' class triggers Gumby\'s design updates to the select (making multi-selects appear like drop down selects) so instead I think a new class of \'multi-picker\' could help and be used as the wrapper for multi-selects instead of \'picker\'.\r\n\r\nSelect "Picker" Example:\r\n&lt;div class="picker"&gt;\r\n    &lt;select&gt;\r\n        &lt;option value="#" disabled=""&gt;Favorite Dalek phrase...&lt;/option&gt;\r\n        &lt;option&gt;EXTERMINATE&lt;/option&gt;\r\n        &lt;option&gt;EXTERMINATE&lt;/option&gt;\r\n        &lt;option&gt;EXTERMINATE&lt;/option&gt;\r\n    &lt;/select&gt;\r\n&lt;/div&gt;\r\n\r\nSelect "Multi-Picker" Example:\r\n&lt;div class="multi-picker"&gt;\r\n    &lt;select multiple="multiple"&gt;\r\n        &lt;option value="#" disabled=""&gt;Favorite Dalek phrase...&lt;/option&gt;\r\n        &lt;option&gt;EXTERMINATE&lt;/option&gt;\r\n        &lt;option&gt;EXTERMINATE&lt;/option&gt;\r\n        &lt;option&gt;EXTERMINATE&lt;/option&gt;\r\n    &lt;/select&gt;\r\n&lt;/div&gt;\r\n\r\nThe proposed styles attempt to use many of the same styles already used in Gumby\'s UI for &lt;select&gt;
